### [393] [A Kernel Nonconformity Score for Multivariate Conformal Prediction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.21595)
*Louis Meyer,Wenkai Xu*

Main category: stat.ML

Relevance: 10.0

TL;DR: 提出了一种多变量核评分（MKS）方法，用于多变量共形预测，该评分能显式适应残差分布的几何结构，同时统一了贝叶斯不确定性量化与频率学派覆盖保证。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 多变量共形预测需要将残差向量压缩为标量的非一致评分，同时保留残差分布的隐式几何结构，现有方法在这方面存在不足。

Method: 提出多变量核评分（MKS），其类似高斯过程后验方差，可分解为各向异性最大平均差异（MMD），在核密度估计与协方差加权距离之间插值。

Result: 证明了有限样本覆盖保证和收敛速率，收敛性取决于核协方差算子的有效秩而非维度；在回归任务中，与椭球基线相比，显著减小了预测区域体积，在高维和更紧覆盖水平下增益更大。

Conclusion: MKS实现了维度无关的自适应，为多变量共形预测提供了更高效、几何自适应的预测区域构建方法。

Abstract: Multivariate conformal prediction requires nonconformity scores that compress residual vectors into scalars while preserving certain implicit geometric structure of the residual distribution. We introduce a Multivariate Kernel Score (MKS) that produces prediction regions that explicitly adapt to this geometry. We show that the proposed score resembles the Gaussian process posterior variance, unifying Bayesian uncertainty quantification with the coverage guarantees of frequentist-type. Moreover, the MKS can be decomposed into an anisotropic Maximum Mean Discrepancy (MMD) that interpolates between kernel density estimation and covariance-weighted distance. We prove finite-sample coverage guarantees and establish convergence rates that depend on the effective rank of the kernel-based covariance operator rather than the ambient dimension, enabling dimension-free adaptation. On regression tasks, the MKS reduces the volume of prediction region significantly, compared to ellipsoidal baselines while maintaining nominal coverage, with larger gains at higher dimensions and tighter coverage levels.

</details>


### [394] [A-IC3: Learning-Guided Adaptive Inductive Generalization for Hardware Model Checking](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.21688)
*Xiaofeng Zhou,Guangyu Hu,Hongce Zhang,Wei Zhang*

Main category: cs.LO

Relevance: 10.0

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于多臂老虎机（MAB）的轻量级机器学习框架，用于动态选择IC3硬件模型检测算法中的归纳泛化策略，替代传统的固定策略，从而提升验证效率。在914个基准测试中，该方法在SOTA模型检查器rIC3上比基线多解决26-50个案例，PAR-2分数提升194.72-389.29。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: IC3算法的归纳泛化过程对整体性能至关重要，但现有方法依赖固定的归纳泛化策略，忽视了验证环境的动态性和上下文敏感性，导致生成的子句质量受限，影响算法性能。

Method: 提出轻量级机器学习框架，使用多臂老虎机（MAB）算法根据验证过程的实时反馈动态选择归纳泛化策略，通过评估泛化结果的质量来更新代理，从而随时间优化策略选择。

Result: 在914个实例的基准测试（主要来自最新HWMCC集合）上，该方法在SOTA模型检查器rIC3上比基线多解决26-50个案例，PAR-2分数提升194.72-389.29。

Conclusion: 该动态策略选择框架有效提升了IC3算法的验证效率，证明了轻量级机器学习在硬件模型检测中具有实用价值。

Abstract: The IC3 algorithm represents the state-of-the-art (SOTA) hardware model checking technique, owing to its robust performance and scalability. A significant body of research has focused on enhancing the solving efficiency of the IC3 algorithm, with particular attention to the inductive generalization process: a critical phase wherein the algorithm seeks to generalize a counterexample to inductiveness (CTI), which typically is a state leading to a bad state, into a broader set of states. This inductive generalization is a primary source of clauses in IC3 and thus plays a pivotal role in determining the overall effectiveness of the algorithm.
  Despite its importance, existing approaches often rely on fixed inductive generalization strategies, overlooking the dynamic and context-sensitive nature of the verification environment in which spurious counterexamples arise. This rigidity can limit the quality of generated clauses and, consequently, the performance of IC3.
  To address this limitation, we propose a lightweight machine-learning-based framework that dynamically selects appropriate inductive generalization strategies in response to the evolving verification context. Specifically, we employ a multi-armed bandit (MAB) algorithm to adaptively choose inductive generalization strategies based on real-time feedback from the verification process. The agent is updated by evaluating the quality of generalization outcomes, thereby refining its strategy selection over time.
  Empirical evaluation on a benchmark suite comprising 914 instances, primarily drawn from the latest HWMCC collection, demonstrates the efficacy of our approach. When implemented on the state-of-the-art model checker rIC3, our method solves 26 to 50 more cases than the baselines and improves the PAR-2 score by 194.72 to 389.29.

</details>


### [395] [Beyond Expected Information Gain: Stable Bayesian Optimal Experimental Design with Integral Probability Metrics and Plug-and-Play Extensions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.21849)
*Di Wu,Ling Liang,Haizhao Yang*

Main category: stat.ML

Relevance: 10.0

TL;DR: 本文提出基于积分概率度量（IPM）的贝叶斯最优实验设计（BOED）框架，替代传统基于KL散度的期望信息增益（EIG）方法，解决支撑不匹配、尾部低估等问题，并提供更强的几何感知稳定性和理论保证。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统BOED依赖KL散度定义EIG，存在嵌套期望计算困难、支撑不匹配、尾部低估和罕见事件敏感等根本性问题，尤其在资源受限场景下成为瓶颈。

Method: 提出IPM-based BOED框架，用积分概率度量（Wasserstein距离、最大均值差异、能量距离）替代KL散度，并支持即插即用扩展至神经最优传输等几何感知差异度量。

Result: 理论证明IPM-based效用函数在代理模型误差和先验误设定下具有更强的几何感知稳定性；实验表明能产生高度集中的可信集，在高维场景下优于传统嵌套蒙特卡洛和先进变分方法。

Conclusion: IPM-based BOED框架提供更鲁棒、几何感知的实验设计，有效解决KL-based方法的固有缺陷，在资源受限和高维场景下表现优越。

Abstract: Bayesian Optimal Experimental Design (BOED) provides a rigorous framework for decision-making tasks in which data acquisition is often the critical bottleneck, especially in resource-constrained settings. Traditionally, BOED typically selects designs by maximizing expected information gain (EIG), commonly defined through the Kullback-Leibler (KL) divergence. However, classical evaluation of EIG often involves challenging nested expectations, and even advanced variational methods leave the underlying log-density-ratio objective unchanged. As a result, support mismatch, tail underestimation, and rare-event sensitivity remain intrinsic concerns for KL-based BOED. To address these fundamental bottlenecks, we introduce an IPM-based BOED framework that replaces density-based divergences with integral probability metrics (IPMs), including the Wasserstein distance, Maximum Mean Discrepancy, and Energy Distance, resulting in a highly flexible plug-and-play BOED framework. We establish theoretical guarantees showing that IPM-based utilities provide stronger geometry-aware stability under surrogate-model error and prior misspecification than classical EIG-based utilities. We also validate the proposed framework empirically, demonstrating that IPM-based designs yield highly concentrated credible sets. Furthermore, by extending the same sample-based BOED template in a plug-and-play manner to geometry-aware discrepancies beyond the IPM class, illustrated by a neural optimal transport estimator, we achieve accurate optimal designs in high-dimensional settings where conventional nested Monte Carlo estimators and advanced variational methods fail.

</details>


### [396] [KinetiDiff: Docking-Guided Diffusion for De Novo ACVR1 Inhibitor Design in Fibrodysplasia Ossificans Progressiva](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.20886)
*Aaryan Patel*

Main category: physics.chem-ph

Relevance: 6.0

TL;DR: KinetiDiff是一种结合几何完备扩散模型与AutoDock Vina梯度引导的从头激酶抑制剂设计框架，针对ACVR1（ALK2）激酶生成高亲和力分子。从10,000个样本中产生9,997个有效分子，最佳候选结合能达-11.05 kcal/mol，相比晶体学参考提升19.2%。前100个候选均超过参考，且100%符合Lipinski规则。系统消融实验表明实时对接梯度引导在所有指标上占优。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 针对罕见病激酶靶点（如FOP中的ACVR1/ALK2），现有从头药物设计方法缺乏有效结合物理先验引导，生成的分子亲和力不足。作者希望将扩散模型的生成能力与基于物理的对接打分相结合，实现面向高亲和力构象的定向分子生成。

Method: 提出KinetiDiff框架：1) 采用几何完备扩散模型（Geometry-Complete Diffusion Model）生成分子结构；2) 在扩散去噪循环中注入AutoDock Vina的物理对接梯度，引导生成过程朝向高亲和力构象；3) 对比四种引导策略（Vina-Direct物理引导、HNN-Denovo神经代理引导、多目标引导、无引导）进行系统消融实验。

Result: 10,000个采样中9,997个有效分子；最佳候选-11.05 kcal/mol（pKd=8.10），比参考提升19.2%；前100名均超过参考；100% Lipinski合规；中位合成可及性2.67；内部分散度0.790。Vina-Direct物理引导在所有指标上最优。HNN-Denovo有60倍加速但领域失配问题（与Vina相关性仅r=0.224）。

Conclusion: 建立了梯度引导的几何扩散模型作为生成强效、可合成的罕见病激酶靶点抑制剂的有效方法。物理对接梯度引导优于神经代理方法，未来工作可探索融合二者优势。

Abstract: We present KinetiDiff, a structure-based framework for de novo kinase inhibitor design that integrates a Geometry-Complete Diffusion Model with real-time AutoDock Vina gradient guidance. By injecting physics-based docking gradients into the diffusion denoising loop, KinetiDiff steers molecule generation toward high-affinity conformations for ACVR1 (ALK2), the causative kinase in Fibrodysplasia Ossificans Progressiva. From 10,000 diffusion samples, the framework produced 9,997 valid molecules. The best candidate achieved $-11.05$ kcal/mol (pKd = 8.10), a 19.2% improvement over the crystallographic reference. The top 100 candidates all exceed the reference, with 100% Lipinski compliance, median synthetic accessibility of 2.67, and internal diversity of 0.790. Systematic ablation across four guidance strategies--Vina-Direct (physics), HNN-Denovo (neural proxy), multi-objective, and unguided--demonstrates that real-time docking guidance dominates on all metrics. We evaluate HNN-Denovo as a computationally efficient alternative (60-fold speedup per step), revealing a domain-mismatch limitation (r = 0.224 correlation with Vina) that explains its inferior performance. These results establish gradient-guided geometric diffusion as a practical approach for generating potent, synthetically accessible inhibitors against rare-disease kinase targets.

### [397] [An effective variant of the Hartigan $k$-means algorithm](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.21798)
*François Clément,Stefan Steinerberger*

Main category: cs.LG

Relevance: 5.0

TL;DR: 本文研究了Hartigan算法在k-means聚类中的改进，提出了一种微小变体，可在已有Hartigan方法基础上额外提升2%-5%的聚类质量，且改进幅度随维度或聚类数k增加而增大。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: K-means聚类是经典问题，研究表明Hartigan算法几乎总优于Lloyd算法（典型改进5%-10%），作者希望进一步挖掘Hartigan方法的潜力，通过微小变化获得额外提升。

Method: 在Hartigan算法基础上引入一种极小的变体（论文中具体细节未在摘要中详述），通过实验验证其在各种数据集上的效果。

Result: 该变体在Hartigan算法基础上额外带来2%-5%的改进，且当维度或聚类数k增大时，改进幅度趋于变大。

Conclusion: Hartigan算法在k-means中优于Lloyd算法，而作者提出的微小变体能在此基础上进一步稳定提升聚类质量。

Abstract: The k-means problem is perhaps the classical clustering problem and often synonymous with Lloyd's algorithm (1957). It has become clear that Hartigan's algorithm (1975) gives better results in almost all cases, Telgarsky-Vattani note a typical improvement of $5\%$ -- $10\%$. We point out that a very minor variation of Hartigan's method leads to another $2\%$ -- $5\%$ improvement; the improvement tends to become larger when either dimension or $k$ increase.
